I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Using dynamic styles with StyleX constants from defineConsts
### Describe the issue

When using a dynamic function as a style value in `stylex.create` together with a constants from a StyleX constants file (`defineConsts`), the following error occurs:

```bash
/stylex/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__/main.stylex.js: Invalid pseudo or at-rule.

      68 |       )
      69 |     ) {
    > 70 |       throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
         |             ^
      71 |     }
      72 |     if (conditions.includes(key)) {
      73 |       throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);

      at validateConditionalStyles (src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js:70:13)
      at validateConditionalStyles (src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js:42:9)
      at styleXCreateSet (src/shared/stylex-create.js:57:22)
      at transformStyleXCreate (src/visitors/stylex-create.js:169:19)
      at PluginPass.CallExpression (src/index.js:311:30)
      at call (../../../node_modules/@babel/traverse/src/visitors.ts:303:14)

```

### Expected behavior

Correct style transformation using constants as dynamic styles

### Steps to reproduce

Add styles as in `test case` section

### Test case

```js
// packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/transform-stylex-defineConsts-test.js

test('dynamic styles with StyleX constants', () => {
      const { code, } = transformWithInlineConsts(`
        import * as stylex from '@stylexjs/stylex';
        import { mediaQueries } from './constants.stylex';

        export const styles = stylex.create({
          nodeEnd: (animationDuration) => ({
            transition: {
              [mediaQueries.reduceMotion]: 'none',
              default: \`transform \${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out\`,
            },
          }),
        });
      `);

      expect(code).toMatchInlineSnapshot(`
        "
          // Transformation result
        "
      `);
    });
```

Thanks to @martinbooth for discovering and [reporting](https://github.com/Dwlad90/stylex-swc-plugin/issues/504) this bug

    10	import * as messages from '../messages';
    11	import { isPlainObject } from '../utils/object-utils';
    12	
    13	export function validateNamespace(
    14	  namespace: mixed,
    15	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    16	): void {
    17	  if (!isPlainObject(namespace)) {
    18	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_NAMESPACE_VALUE);
    19	  }
    20	  const ns: { +[string]: mixed } = namespace;
    21	  for (const key in ns) {
    22	    const val = ns[key];
    23	    if (val === null || typeof val === 'string' || typeof val === 'number') {
    24	      continue;
    25	    }
    26	    if (Array.isArray(val)) {
    27	      for (const v of val) {
    28	        if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    29	          continue;
    30	        }
    31	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_ARRAY_VALUE);
    32	      }
    33	      continue;
    34	    }
    35	    if (isPlainObject(val)) {
    36	      if (key.startsWith('@') || key.startsWith(':')) {
    37	        if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    38	          throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    39	        }
    40	        validateNamespace(val, [...conditions, key]);
    41	      } else {
    42	        validateConditionalStyles(val as $FlowFixMe);
    43	      }
    44	      continue;
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    48	  }
    49	}
    50	
    51	type ConditionalStyles = $ReadOnly<{
    52	  [key: string]: string | number | ConditionalStyles,
    53	}>;
    54	
    55	function validateConditionalStyles(
    56	  val: ConditionalStyles,
    57	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    58	): void {
    59	  for (const key in val) {
    60	    const v = val[key];
    61	    if (
    62	      !(
    63	        key.startsWith('@') ||
    64	        key.startsWith(':') ||
    65	        // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
    66	        key.startsWith('var(--') ||
    67	        key === 'default'
    68	      )
    69	    ) {
    70	      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
    71	    }
    72	    if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    73	      throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    74	    }
    75	    if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    76	      continue;
    77	    }
    78	    if (Array.isArray(v)) {
    79	      for (const vv of v) {
    80	        if (vv === null || typeof vv === 'string' || typeof vv === 'number') {
    81	          continue;
    82	        }
    83	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    84	      }
    85	      continue;
    86	    }
    87	    if (isPlainObject(v)) {
    88	      validateConditionalStyles(v, [...conditions, key]);
    89	      continue;
    90	    }
    91	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    92	  }
    93	}
    94

     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.
     3	 *

    10	import type { InjectableConstStyle, StyleXOptions } from './common-types';
    11	import type { ConstsConfig } from './stylex-consts-utils';
    12	
    13	import { defaultOptions } from './utils/default-options';
    14	import * as messages from './messages';
    15	
    16	import createHash from './hash';
    17	
    18	export default function styleXDefineConsts<Vars: ConstsConfig>(
    19	  constants: Vars,
    20	  options: $ReadOnly<{ ...Partial<StyleXOptions>, exportId: string, ... }>,
    21	): [
    22	  { [string]: string | number }, // jsOutput JS output
    23	  { [string]: InjectableConstStyle }, // metadata for registerinjectableStyles
    24	] {
    25	  const { classNamePrefix, exportId, debug, enableDebugClassNames } = {
    26	    ...defaultOptions,
    27	    ...options,
    28	  };
    29	
    30	  const jsOutput: { [string]: string | number } = {};
    31	  const injectableStyles: { [string]: InjectableConstStyle } = {};
    32	
    33	  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(constants)) {
    34	    if (key.startsWith('--')) {
    35	      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_CONST_KEY);
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    const varSafeKey = (
    39	      key[0] >= '0' && key[0] <= '9' ? `_${key}` : key
    40	    ).replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_');
    41	
    42	    const constKey =
    43	      debug && enableDebugClassNames
    44	        ? `${varSafeKey}-${classNamePrefix}${createHash(`${exportId}.${key}`)}`
    45	        : `${classNamePrefix}${createHash(`${exportId}.${key}`)}`;
    46	
    47	    jsOutput[key] = value;
    48	    injectableStyles[constKey] = {
    49	      constKey,
    50	      constVal: value,
    51	      priority: 0,
    52	      ltr: '',
    53	      rtl: null,
    54	    };
    55	  }
    56	
    57	  return [jsOutput, injectableStyles];
    58	}

     1	/**
     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.
     3	 *
     4	 * This source code is licensed under the MIT license found in the
     5	 * LICENSE file in the root directory of this source tree.
     6	 *
     7	 * @flow strict
     8	 */
     9	
    10	import type { NodePath } from '@babel/traverse';
    11	
    12	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    13	import { evaluate } from '../utils/evaluate-path';
    14	import { utils, defineConsts as styleXDefineConsts, messages } from '../shared';
    15	import { convertObjectToAST } from '../utils/js-to-ast';
    16	import StateManager from '../utils/state-manager';
    17	
    18	/// This function looks for `stylex.defineConsts` calls and transforms them.
    19	/// 1. It finds and validates the first argument to `stylex.defineConsts`.
    20	/// 2. It evaluates the style const object to a JS value, erroring on non-static or non-object values.
    21	/// 3. It generates a theme name from the filename and export name for hashing.
    22	/// 4. It invokes `stylexDefineConsts` to transform the JS object and collect injected styles.
    23	/// 5. It creates a map of key-value pairs of constants to be inlined.
    24	/// 6. It replaces the call with the transformed AST and registers the styles in state.
    25	export default function transformStyleXDefineConsts(
    26	  callExpressionPath: NodePath<t.CallExpression>,
    27	  state: StateManager,
    28	) {
    29	  const callExpressionNode = callExpressionPath.node;
    30	  if (callExpressionNode.type !== 'CallExpression') return;
    31	
    32	  if (
    33	    (callExpressionNode.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
    34	      state.stylexDefineConstsImport.has(callExpressionNode.callee.name)) ||
    35	    (callExpressionNode.callee.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
    36	      callExpressionNode.callee.property.name === 'defineConsts' &&
    37	      callExpressionNode.callee.object.type === 'Identifier' &&
    38	      state.stylexImport.has(callExpressionNode.callee.object.name))
    39	  ) {
    40	    validateStyleXDefineConsts(callExpressionPath);
    41	
    42	    const variableDeclaratorPath = callExpressionPath.parentPath;
    43	    if (!variableDeclaratorPath.isVariableDeclarator()) return;
    44	
    45	    const variableDeclaratorNode = variableDeclaratorPath.node;
    46	    if (variableDeclaratorNode.id.type !== 'Identifier') return;
    47	
    48	    const varId: t.Identifier = variableDeclaratorNode.id;
    49	    const args = callExpressionPath.get('arguments');
    50	    const firstArg = args[0];
    51	
    52	    const { confident, value } = evaluate(firstArg, state);
    53	    if (!confident) {
    54	      throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
    55	        messages.nonStaticValue('defineConsts'),
    56	        SyntaxError,
    57	      );
    58	    }
    59	    if (typeof value !== 'object' || value == null) {
    60	      throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
    61	        messages.nonStyleObject('defineConsts'),
    62	        SyntaxError,
    63	      );
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    const fileName = state.fileNameForHashing;
    67	    if (fileName == null) {
    68	      throw new Error(messages.cannotGenerateHash('defineConsts'));
    69	    }
    70	
    71	    const exportName = varId.name;
    72	    const exportId = utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName });
    73	
    74	    const [transformedJsOutput, jsOutput] = styleXDefineConsts(value, {
    75	      ...state.options,
    76	      exportId,
    77	    });
    78	
    79	    callExpressionPath.replaceWith(convertObjectToAST(transformedJsOutput));
    80	
    81	    const styles = Object.entries(jsOutput).map(([_, obj]) => [
    82	      obj.constKey,
    83	      {
    84	        constKey: obj.constKey,
    85	        constVal: obj.constVal,
    86	        ltr: obj.ltr,
    87	        rtl: obj.rtl ?? null,
    88	      },
    89	      obj.priority,
    90	    ]);
    91	
    92	    state.registerStyles(styles);
    93	  }
    94	}
    95	
    96	function validateStyleXDefineConsts(
    97	  callExpressionPath: NodePath<t.CallExpression>,
    98	) {
    99	  const variableDeclaratorPath = callExpressionPath.parentPath;
   100	  const exportNamedDeclarationPath =
   101	    variableDeclaratorPath.parentPath?.parentPath;
   102	
   103	  if (
   104	    variableDeclaratorPath == null ||
   105	    !variableDeclaratorPath.isVariableDeclarator() ||
   106	    variableDeclaratorPath.node.id.type !== 'Identifier'
   107	  ) {
   108	    throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
   109	      messages.unboundCallValue('defineConsts'),
   110	      SyntaxError,
   111	    );
   112	  }
   113	
   114	  if (
   115	    exportNamedDeclarationPath == null ||
   116	    !exportNamedDeclarationPath.isExportNamedDeclaration()
   117	  ) {
   118	    throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
   119	      messages.nonExportNamedDeclaration('defineConsts'),
   120	      SyntaxError,
   121	    );
   122	  }
   123	
   124	  if (callExpressionPath.node.arguments.length !== 1) {
   125	    throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
   126	      messages.illegalArgumentLength('defineConsts', 1),
   127	      SyntaxError,
   128	    );
   129	  }
   130	}
   131

    36	function isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr: t.Expression): boolean {
    37	  if (t.isTemplateLiteral(expr)) return true;
    38	
    39	  if (
    40	    t.isStringLiteral(expr) ||
    41	    t.isNumericLiteral(expr) ||
    42	    t.isBooleanLiteral(expr)
    43	  )
    44	    return true;
    45	
    46	  if (t.isBinaryExpression(expr)) {
    47	    return ['+', '-', '*', '/', '%', '**'].includes(expr.operator);
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  if (t.isUnaryExpression(expr)) {
    51	    return ['-', '+'].includes(expr.operator);
    52	  }
    53	
    54	  if (t.isConditionalExpression(expr)) {
    55	    return (
    56	      isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.consequent) &&
    57	      isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.alternate)
    58	    );
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  if (t.isLogicalExpression(expr)) {
    62	    if (expr.operator === '??' || expr.operator === '||') {
    63	      return (
    64	        isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.left) || isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.right)
    65	      );
    66	    }
    67	    if (expr.operator === '&&') {
    68	      return (
    69	        isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.left) && isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.right)
    70	      );
    71	    }
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  return false;
    75	}

    77	/// This function looks for `stylex.create` calls and transforms them.
    78	/// 1. It finds the first argument to `stylex.create` and validates it.
    79	/// 2. It pre-processes valid-dynamic parts of style object such as custom presets (spreads)
    80	/// 3. It evaluates the style object to get a JS object. This also handles local constants automatically.
    81	/// 4. It uses the `stylexCreate` from `@stylexjs/shared` to transform the JS
    82	///    object and to get a list of injected styles.
    83	/// 5. It converts the resulting Object back into an AST and replaces the call with it.
    84	/// 6. It also inserts `stylex.inject` calls above the current statement as needed.
    85	export default function transformStyleXCreate(
    86	  path: NodePath<t.CallExpression>,
    87	  state: StateManager,
    88	) {
    89	  const { node } = path;
    90	
    91	  if (node.type !== 'CallExpression') {
    92	    return;
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  if (
    96	    (node.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
    97	      state.stylexCreateImport.has(node.callee.name)) ||
    98	    (node.callee.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
    99	      node.callee.object.type === 'Identifier' &&
   100	      node.callee.property.type === 'Identifier' &&
   101	      node.callee.property.name === 'create' &&
   102	      state.stylexImport.has(node.callee.object.name))
   103	  ) {
   104	    validateStyleXCreate(path);

   112	      >,
   113	    > = path.get('arguments');
   114	    const firstArg = args[0];
   115

   118	    const otherInjectedCSSRules: { [propertyName: string]: InjectableStyle } =
   119	      {};

   122	    function keyframes<
   123	      Obj: {

   125	      },

   127	      const [animationName, injectedStyle] = stylexKeyframes(

   129	        state.options,

   134

   136	    function positionTry<

   153	    });
   154	    state.stylexKeyframesImport.forEach((name) => {
   155	      identifiers[name] = { fn: keyframes };
   156	    });

   159	    });

   161	      if (memberExpressions[name] == null) {

   163	      }
   164	      memberExpressions[name].firstThatWorks = { fn: stylexFirstThatWorks };
   165	      memberExpressions[name].keyframes = { fn: keyframes };
   166	      memberExpressions[name].positionTry = { fn: positionTry };
   167	    });
   168	
   169	    const { confident, value, fns, reason, deopt } = evaluateStyleXCreateArg(
   170	      firstArg,
   171	      state,

   173	        identifiers,

   176	    );
   177

   179	      throw (deopt ?? path).buildCodeFrameError(

   181	        SyntaxError,

   236	    }

   241	    }
   242	
   243	    if (varName != null) {

   245	      state.styleMap.set(varName, stylesToRemember);
   246	      state.styleVars.set(varName, path.parentPath as $FlowFixMe);

   400	              prop.value = t.arrowFunctionExpression(params, finalFnValue);
   401	            }
   402	          }
   403	        }
   404	
   405	        return prop;
   406	      });
   407	    }
   408	
   409	    const listOfStyles = Object.entries(injectedStyles).map(
   410	      ([key, { priority, ...rest }]) => [key, rest, priority],
   411	    );
   412	
   413	    state.registerStyles(listOfStyles, path);
   414	
   415	    pathReplaceHoisted(path, resultAst);
   416	
   417	    if (Object.keys(injectedStyles).length === 0) {
   418	      return;
   419	    }
   420	  }

    11	import type { NodePath } from '@babel/traverse';

    15	import StateManager from '../utils/state-manager';

    20	  timeUnits,

    25	type TInlineStyles = {
    26	  [string]: {
    27	    +path: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    28	    +originalExpression: t.Expression,
    29	    +expression: t.Expression | t.PatternLike,
    30	  },
    31	};
    32	
    33	type DynamicFns = {
    34	  [string]: [
    35	    +params: Array<t.Identifier>,
    36	    +inlineStyles: $ReadOnly<TInlineStyles>,
    37	  ],
    38	};
    39	
    40	// This
    41	export function evaluateStyleXCreateArg(
    42	  path: NodePath<>,
    43	  traversalState: StateManager,
    44	  functions: FunctionConfig = { identifiers: {}, memberExpressions: {} },
    45	): $ReadOnly<{
    46	  confident: boolean,
    47	  value: any,
    48	  deopt?: null | NodePath<>,
    49	  reason?: string,
    50	  fns?: DynamicFns,
    51	}> {
    52	  if (!path.isObjectExpression()) {
    53	    return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    54	  }
    55	
    56	  const value: { [string]: mixed } = {};
    57	  const fns: DynamicFns = {};
    58	
    59	  for (const prop of path.get('properties')) {
    60	    if (!prop.isObjectProperty()) {
    61	      return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    62	    }
    63	    const objPropPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty> = prop;
    64	    const keyResult = evaluateObjKey(objPropPath, traversalState, functions);
    65	    if (!keyResult.confident) {
    66	      return { confident: false, deopt: keyResult.deopt, value: null };
    67	    }
    68	    const key = keyResult.value;
    69	
    70	    const valPath = prop.get('value');
    71	    if (!valPath.isArrowFunctionExpression()) {
    72	      const val = evaluate(valPath, traversalState, functions);
    73	      if (!val.confident) {
    74	        return val;
    75	      }
    76	      value[key] = val.value;
    77	      continue;
    78	    }
    79	    const fnPath: NodePath<t.ArrowFunctionExpression> = valPath;
    80	    const allParams: Array<
    81	      NodePath<t.Identifier | t.SpreadElement | t.Pattern>,
    82	    > = fnPath.get('params');
    83	
    84	    validateDynamicStyleParams(fnPath, allParams);
    85	
    86	    const params: Array<t.Identifier> = allParams
    87	      .filter(
    88	        (
    89	          param: NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.SpreadElement>,
    90	        ): param is NodePath<t.Identifier> => param.isIdentifier(),
    91	      )
    92	      .map((param) => param.node);
    93	
    94	    const fnBody = fnPath.get('body');
    95	    if (!fnBody.isObjectExpression()) {
    96	      // We only allow arrow functions without block bodies.
    97	      return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    98	    }
    99	    const fnObjectBody: NodePath<t.ObjectExpression> = fnBody;
   100	    const evalResult = evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   101	      fnObjectBody,
   102	      traversalState,
   103	      functions,
   104	    );
   105	
   106	    if (!evalResult.confident) {
   107	      const { confident, value: v, deopt } = evalResult;
   108	      return { confident, value: v, deopt };
   109	    }
   110	    const { value: v, inlineStyles } = evalResult;
   111	    value[key] = v;
   112	    fns[key] = [params, inlineStyles ?? {}];
   113	  }
   114	
   115	  return { value, confident: true, fns };
   116	}
   117	
   118	function evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   119	  path: NodePath<t.ObjectExpression>,
   120	  traversalState: StateManager,
   121	  functions: FunctionConfig = { identifiers: {}, memberExpressions: {} },
   122	  keyPath: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
   123	): $ReadOnly<{
   124	  confident: boolean,
   125	  value: any,
   126	  deopt?: null | NodePath<>,
   127	  reason?: string,
   128	  inlineStyles?: $ReadOnly<TInlineStyles>,
   129	}> {
   130	  const obj: { [string]: mixed } = {};
   131	  const inlineStyles: TInlineStyles = {};
   132	  const props: $ReadOnlyArray<
   133	    NodePath<t.ObjectMethod | t.ObjectProperty | t.SpreadElement>,
   134	  > = path.get('properties');
   135	  for (const prop of props) {
   136	    if (prop.isObjectMethod()) {
   137	      return { value: null, confident: false };
   138	    }
   139	    if (prop.isSpreadElement()) {
   140	      const result = evaluate(prop.get('argument'), traversalState, functions);
   141	      if (!result.confident) {
   142	        return result;
   143	      }
   144	      Object.assign(obj, result.value);
   145	      continue;
   146	    }
   147	    if (prop.isObjectProperty()) {
   148	      const keyResult = evaluateObjKey(prop, traversalState, functions);
   149	      if (!keyResult.confident) {
   150	        return { confident: false, deopt: keyResult.deopt, value: null };
   151	      }
   152	      let key = keyResult.value;
   153	      if (key.startsWith('var(') && key.endsWith(')')) {
   154	        key = key.slice(4, -1);
   155	      }
   156	
   157	      const valuePath: NodePath<t.Expression | t.PatternLike> =
   158	        prop.get('value');
   159	
   160	      if (valuePath.isObjectExpression()) {
   161	        const result = evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   162	          valuePath,
   163	          traversalState,
   164	          functions,
   165	          [...keyPath, key],
   166	        );
   167	        if (!result.confident) {
   168	          return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt, value: null };
   169	        }
   170	        obj[key] = result.value;
   171	        Object.assign(inlineStyles, result.inlineStyles);
   172	      } else {
   173	        const result = evaluate(valuePath, traversalState, functions);
   174	        if (!result.confident) {
   175	          const fullKeyPath = [...keyPath, key];
   176	          const varName =
   177	            '--x-' +
   178	            (keyPath.length > 0
   179	              ? utils.hash([...keyPath, key].join('_'))
   180	              : key);
   181	          obj[key] = `var(${varName})`;
   182	          const node = valuePath.node;
   183	          if (!t.isExpression(node)) {
   184	            throw valuePath.buildCodeFrameError(
   185	              'Expected expression as style value',
   186	              SyntaxError,
   187	            );
   188	          }
   189	          const expression: t.Expression = node as $FlowFixMe;
   190	
   191	          const propName =
   192	            fullKeyPath.find(
   193	              (k) =>
   194	                !k.startsWith(':') && !k.startsWith('@') && k !== 'default',
   195	            ) ?? key;
   196	
   197	          const unit =
   198	            timeUnits.has(propName) || lengthUnits.has(propName)
   199	              ? getNumberSuffix(propName)
   200	              : '';
   201	
   202	          const inlineStyleExpression =
   203	            unit !== ''
   204	              ? t.callExpression(
   205	                  t.arrowFunctionExpression(
   206	                    [t.identifier('val')],
   207	                    t.conditionalExpression(
   208	                      t.binaryExpression(
   209	                        '===',
   210	                        t.unaryExpression('typeof', t.identifier('val')),
   211	                        t.stringLiteral('number'),
   212	                      ),
   213	                      t.binaryExpression(
   214	                        '+',
   215	                        t.identifier('val'),
   216	                        t.stringLiteral(unit),
   217	                      ),
   218	                      t.conditionalExpression(
   219	                        t.binaryExpression(
   220	                          '!=',
   221	                          t.identifier('val'),
   222	                          t.nullLiteral(),
   223	                        ),
   224	                        t.identifier('val'),
   225	                        t.identifier('undefined'),
   226	                      ),
   227	                    ),
   228	                  ),
   229	                  [expression as t.Expression],
   230	                )
   231	              : t.conditionalExpression(
   232	                  t.binaryExpression('!=', expression, t.nullLiteral()),
   233	                  expression,
   234	                  t.identifier('undefined'),
   235	                );
   236	          inlineStyles[varName] = {
   237	            path: [...keyPath, key],
   238	            originalExpression: expression,
   239	            expression: inlineStyleExpression,
   240	          };
   241	        } else {
   242	          obj[key] = result.value;
   243	        }
   244	      }
   245	    }
   246	  }
   247	  return { value: obj, confident: true, inlineStyles };
   248	}
   249	
   250	type KeyResult =
   251	  | { confident: true, value: string }
   252	  | { confident: false, deopt?: null | NodePath<> };
   253	
   254	function evaluateObjKey(
   255	  prop: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty>,
   256	  traversalState: StateManager,
   257	  functions: FunctionConfig,
   258	): KeyResult {
   259	  const keyPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty['key']> = prop.get('key');
   260	  let key: string;
   261	  if ((prop.node as t.ObjectProperty).computed) {
   262	    const result = evaluate(keyPath, traversalState, functions);
   263	    if (!result.confident) {
   264	      return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt };
   265	    }
   266	    key = result.value;
   267	  } else if (keyPath.isIdentifier()) {
   268	    key = keyPath.node.name;
   269	  } else {
   270	    // TODO: This is'nt handling all possible types that `keyPath` could be
   271	    key = (keyPath.node as $FlowFixMe).value;
   272	  }
   273	  return {
   274	    confident: true,
   275	    value: String(key),
   276	  };
   277	}
   278	
   279	function validateDynamicStyleParams(
   280	  path: NodePath<t.ArrowFunctionExpression>,
   281	  params: Array<NodePath<t.Identifier | t.SpreadElement | t.Pattern>>,
   282	) {
   283	  if (params.some((param) => !param.isIdentifier())) {
   284	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   285	      messages.ONLY_NAMED_PARAMETERS_IN_DYNAMIC_STYLE_FUNCTIONS,
   286	      SyntaxError,
   287	    );
   288	  }
   289	}

    21	
    22	function transform(source, opts = {}) {
    23	  const { code, metadata } = transformSync(source, {
    24	    filename: opts.filename || '/stylex/packages/TestTheme.stylex.js',
    25	    parserOpts: {
    26	      flow: 'all',
    27	    },
    28	    babelrc: false,
    29	    plugins: [
    30	      [
    31	        stylexPlugin,
    32	        {
    33	          ...defaultOpts,
    34	          ...opts,
    35	        },
    36	      ],
    37	    ],
    38	  });
    39	  return { code, metadata };
    40	}
    41	
    42	function transformWithInlineConsts(source, opts = {}) {
    43	  const { code, metadata } = transformSync(source, {
    44	    filename: path.join(__dirname, '__fixtures__/main.stylex.js'),
    45	    parserOpts: { sourceType: 'module' },
    46	    babelrc: false,
    47	    plugins: [
    48	      [

    50	        {
    51	          ...opts,
    52	          unstable_moduleResolution: {
    53	            rootDir: path.join(__dirname, '__fixtures__'),
    54	            type: 'commonJS',
    55	          },
    56	        },
    57	      ],
    58	    ],
    59	  });
    60	
    61	  return { code, metadata };
    62	}

     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.
     3	 *

    10	/**
    11	 * This is a extended version of the path evaluation code from Babel.
    12	 *
    13	 * The original can be found at:
    14	 * https://github.com/babel/babel/blob/main/packages/babel-traverse/src/path/evaluation.ts
    15	 *
    16	 * The following extensions were made:
    17	 * - It can accept a mapping from variable names to functions
    18	 *   which when encountered will be evaluated instead of deopting.
    19	 *   - The functions can be configured to accept the raw path instead of
    20	 *     static values to handle dynamic values.
    21	 * - It can handle object spreads when the spread value itself is statically evaluated.
    22	 */
    23	
    24	import type { NodePath, Binding } from '@babel/traverse';
    25	
    26	import { parseSync } from '@babel/core';
    27	import traverse from '@babel/traverse';
    28	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    29	import StateManager from './state-manager';
    30	import { utils } from '../shared';
    31	import * as errMsgs from './evaluation-errors';
    32	
    33	// This file contains Babels metainterpreter that can evaluate static code.
    34	
    35	const VALID_CALLEES = ['String', 'Number', 'Math', 'Object', 'Array'];
    36	const INVALID_METHODS = [
    37	  'random',
    38	  'assign',
    39	  'defineProperties',
    40	  'defineProperty',
    41	  'freeze',
    42	  'seal',
    43	  'splice',
    44	];
    45	
    46	function isValidCallee(val: string): boolean {
    47	  return (VALID_CALLEES as $ReadOnlyArray<string>).includes(val);
    48	}
    49	
    50	function isInvalidMethod(val: string): boolean {
    51	  return INVALID_METHODS.includes(val);
    52	}
    53	
    54	export type FunctionConfig = {
    55	  identifiers: {
    56	    [fnName: string]: $FlowFixMe,
    57	  },
    58	  memberExpressions: {
    59	    [key: string]: {
    60	      [memberName: string]: {
    61	        fn: (...args: $FlowFixMe[]) => $FlowFixMe,
    62	        takesPath?: boolean,
    63	      },
    64	    },
    65	  },
    66	};
    67	
    68	type State = {
    69	  confident: boolean,
    70	  deoptPath: NodePath<> | null,
    71	  deoptReason?: string,
    72	  seen: Map<t.Node, Result>,
    73	  addedImports: Set<string>,
    74	  functions: FunctionConfig,
    75	  traversalState: StateManager,
    76	};
    77	
    78	type Result =
    79	  | {
    80	      resolved: true,
    81	      value: any,
    82	    }
    83	  | {
    84	      resolved: false,
    85	      reason: string,
    86	    };
    87	/**
    88	 * Deopts the evaluation
    89	 */
    90	function deopt(path: NodePath<>, state: State, reason: string): void {
    91	  if (!state.confident) return;
    92	  state.deoptPath = path;
    93	  state.confident = false;
    94	  state.deoptReason = reason;
    95	}
    96	
    97	function evaluateImportedFile(
    98	  filePath: string,
    99	  namedExport: string,
   100	  state: State,
   101	  bindingPath: NodePath<>,
   102	): any {
   103	  const fs = require('fs');
   104	  const fileContents = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   105	  // It's safe to use `.babelrc` here because we're only
   106	  // interested in the JS runtime, and not the CSS.
   107	  // TODO: in environments where `.babelrc` is not available,
   108	  // we need to find a way to decide whether to use Flow or TS syntax extensions.
   109	  const ast: null | t.File | { +errors: mixed } = parseSync(fileContents, {
   110	    babelrc: true,
   111	  });
   112	  if (!ast || ast.errors || !t.isNode(ast)) {
   113	    deopt(bindingPath, state, errMsgs.IMPORT_FILE_PARSING_ERROR);
   114	    return;
   115	  }
   116	
   117	  const astNode: t.Node = ast as $FlowFixMe;
   118	
   119	  let result: any;
   120	
   121	  traverse(astNode, {
   122	    ExportNamedDeclaration(path: NodePath<t.ExportNamedDeclaration>) {
   123	      const declaration = path.get('declaration');
   124	
   125	      if (declaration.isVariableDeclaration()) {
   126	        const decls = declaration.get('declarations');
   127	
   128	        const finder = (decl: NodePath<t.Node>) => {
   129	          if (decl.isVariableDeclarator()) {
   130	            const id = decl.get('id');
   131	            const init: ?NodePath<t.Expression> = (
   132	              decl as NodePath<t.VariableDeclarator>
   133	            ).get('init');
   134	            if (
   135	              id.isIdentifier() &&
   136	              id.node.name === namedExport &&
   137	              init != null &&
   138	              init.isExpression()
   139	            ) {
   140	              result = evaluateCached(init, state);
   141	            }
   142	          }
   143	        };
   144	        if (Array.isArray(decls)) {
   145	          decls.forEach(finder);
   146	        } else {
   147	          finder(decls);
   148	        }
   149	      }
   150	    },
   151	  });
   152	
   153	  if (state.confident) {
   154	    return result;
   155	  } else {
   156	    deopt(bindingPath, state, errMsgs.IMPORT_FILE_EVAL_ERROR);
   157	    return;
   158	  }
   159	}
   160	
   161	function evaluateThemeRef(
   162	  fileName: string,
   163	  exportName: string,
   164	  state: State,
   165	): { [key: string]: string } {
   166	  const resolveKey = (key: string) => {
   167	    if (key.startsWith('--')) {
   168	      return `var(${key})`;
   169	    }
   170	
   171	    const strToHash =
   172	      key === '__varGroupHash__'
   173	        ? utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName })
   174	        : utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName, key });
   175	
   176	    const { debug, enableDebugClassNames } = state.traversalState.options;
   177	
   178	    const varSafeKey =
   179	      key === '__varGroupHash__'
   180	        ? ''
   181	        : (key[0] >= '0' && key[0] <= '9' ? `_${key}` : key).replace(
   182	            /[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,
   183	            '_',
   184	          ) + '-';
   185	
   186	    const varName =
   187	      debug && enableDebugClassNames
   188	        ? varSafeKey +
   189	          state.traversalState.options.classNamePrefix +
   190	          utils.hash(strToHash)
   191	        : state.traversalState.options.classNamePrefix + utils.hash(strToHash);
   192	
   193	    if (key === '__varGroupHash__') {
   194	      return varName;
   195	    }
   196	    return `var(--${varName})`;
   197	  };
   198	
   199	  // A JS proxy that uses the key to generate a string value using the `resolveKey` function
   200	  const proxy = new Proxy(
   201	    {},
   202	    {
   203	      get(_, key: string) {
   204	        return resolveKey(key);
   205	      },
   206	      set(_, key: string, value: string) {
   207	        throw new Error(
   208	          `Cannot set value ${value} to key ${key} in theme ${fileName}`,
   209	        );
   210	      },
   211	    },
   212	  );
   213	
   214	  return proxy;
   215	}
   216	
   217	/**
   218	 * We wrap the _evaluate method so we can track `seen` nodes, we push an item
   219	 * to the map before we actually evaluate it so we can deopt on self recursive
   220	 * nodes such as:
   221	 *
   222	 *   var g = a ? 1 : 2,
   223	 *       a = g * this.foo
   224	 */
   225	function evaluateCached(path: NodePath<>, state: State): any {
   226	  const { node } = path;
   227	  const { seen } = state;
   228	
   229	  const existing: ?Result = seen.get(node);
   230	  if (existing != null) {
   231	    if (existing.resolved) {
   232	      return existing.value;
   233	    } else {
   234	      deopt(path, state, existing.reason);
   235	      return;
   236	    }
   237	  } else {
   238	    const item: Result = { resolved: false, reason: 'Currently evaluating' };
   239	    seen.set(node, item);
   240	
   241	    if (node == null) {
   242	      deopt(path, state, errMsgs.PATH_WITHOUT_NODE);
   243	      return;
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    const val = _evaluate(path, state);
   247	    if (state.confident) {
   248	      seen.set(node, {
   249	        resolved: true,
   250	        value: val,
   251	      });
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    return val;
   255	  }
   256	}
   257	
   258	function _evaluate(path: NodePath<>, state: State): any {
   259	  if (!state.confident) return;
   260

   258	function _evaluate(path: NodePath<>, state: State): any {
   259	  if (!state.confident) return;
   260	
   261	  if (path.isArrowFunctionExpression()) {
   262	    const body = path.get('body');
   263	    const params: $ReadOnlyArray<
   264	      NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.RestElement>,
   265	    > = path.get('params');
   266	    const identParams = params
   267	      .filter(
   268	        (
   269	          param: NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.RestElement>,
   270	        ): param is NodePath<t.Identifier> => param.isIdentifier(),
   271	      )
   272	      .map((paramPath) => paramPath.node.name);
   273	    if (body.isExpression() && identParams.length === params.length) {
   274	      const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = body;
   275	      return (...args) => {
   276	        const identifierEntries = identParams.map(
   277	          (ident, index): [string, any] => [ident, args[index]],
   278	        );
   279	        const identifiersObj = Object.fromEntries(identifierEntries);
   280	        const result = evaluate(expr, state.traversalState, {
   281	          ...state.functions,
   282	          identifiers: { ...state.functions.identifiers, ...identifiersObj },
   283	        });
   284	        return result.value;
   285	      };
   286	    }
   287	  }
   288	
   289	  if (path.isIdentifier()) {
   290	    const name: string = path.node.name;
   291	    if (Object.keys(state.functions?.identifiers ?? {}).includes(name)) {
   292	      return state.functions.identifiers[name];
   293	    }
   294	  }
   295	
   296	  if (path.isTSAsExpression()) {
   297	    const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = path.get('expression');
   298	    return evaluateCached(expr, state);
   299	  }
   300	
   301	  if (path.node.type === 'TSSatisfiesExpression') {
   302	    const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = (path as $FlowFixMe).get('expression');
   303	    return evaluateCached(expr, state);
   304	  }
   305	
   306	  if (path.isSequenceExpression()) {
   307	    const exprs = path.get('expressions');
   308	    return evaluateCached(exprs[exprs.length - 1], state);
   309	  }
   310	
   311	  if (
   312	    path.isStringLiteral() ||
   313	    path.isNumericLiteral() ||
   314	    path.isBooleanLiteral()
   315	  ) {
   316	    return path.node.value;
   317	  }
   318	
   319	  if (path.isNullLiteral()) {
   320	    return null;
   321	  }
   322	
   323	  if (path.isTemplateLiteral()) {
   324	    return evaluateQuasis(path, path.node.quasis, state);
   325	  }
   326	
   327	  const maybeTag = path.isTaggedTemplateExpression() && path.get('tag');
   328	  if (
   329	    path.isTaggedTemplateExpression() &&
   330	    maybeTag &&
   331	    maybeTag.isMemberExpression()
   332	  ) {
   333	    const tag: NodePath<t.MemberExpression> = maybeTag;
   334	    const object: NodePath<t.Expression | t.Super> = tag.get('object');
   335	
   336	    if (object.isIdentifier()) {
   337	      const name = object.node.name;
   338	      const property: NodePath<> = tag.get('property');
   339	
   340	      if (
   341	        name === 'String' &&
   342	        !path.scope.hasBinding(name) &&
   343	        property.isIdentifier() &&
   344	        property.node.name === 'raw'
   345	      ) {
   346	        return evaluateQuasis(path, path.node.quasi.quasis, state, true);
   347	      }
   348	    }
   349	  }
   350	
   351	  if (path.isConditionalExpression()) {
   352	    const testResult = evaluateCached(path.get('test'), state);
   353	    if (!state.confident) return;
   354	    if (testResult) {
   355	      return evaluateCached(path.get('consequent'), state);
   356	    } else {
   357	      return evaluateCached(path.get('alternate'), state);
   358	    }
   359	  }
   360	
   361	  if (path.isExpressionWrapper()) {
   362	    // TypeCastExpression, ExpressionStatement etc
   363	    return evaluateCached(path.get('expression'), state);
   364	  }
   365	
   366	  // "foo".length
   367	  if (
   368	    path.isMemberExpression() &&
   369	    !path.parentPath.isCallExpression({ callee: path.node })
   370	  ) {
   371	    const object = evaluateCached(path.get('object'), state);
   372	    if (!state.confident) {
   373	      return;
   374	    }
   375	
   376	    const propPath = path.get('property');
   377	
   378	    let property;
   379	    if (path.node.computed) {
   380	      property = evaluateCached(propPath, state);
   381	      if (!state.confident) {
   382	        return;
   383	      }
   384	    } else if (propPath.isIdentifier()) {
   385	      property = propPath.node.name;
   386	    } else if (propPath.isStringLiteral()) {
   387	      property = propPath.node.value;
   388	    } else {
   389	      return deopt(propPath, state, errMsgs.UNEXPECTED_MEMBER_LOOKUP);
   390	    }
   391	
   392	    return object[property];
   393	  }
   394	
   395	  if (path.isReferencedIdentifier()) {
   396	    const binding: ?Binding = path.scope?.getBinding(path.node.name);
   397	
   398	    const bindingPath = binding?.path;
   399	    if (
   400	      binding &&
   401	      bindingPath &&
   402	      !bindingPath.isImportDefaultSpecifier() &&
   403	      !bindingPath.isImportNamespaceSpecifier() &&
   404	      bindingPath.isImportSpecifier()
   405	    ) {
   406	      const importSpecifierPath: NodePath<t.ImportSpecifier> = bindingPath;
   407	      const importSpecifierNode: t.ImportSpecifier = importSpecifierPath.node;
   408	      // const localName = binding.path.node.local.name;
   409	      const imported: t.Identifier | t.StringLiteral =
   410	        importSpecifierNode.imported;
   411	      const importedName =
   412	        imported.type === 'Identifier' ? imported.name : imported.value;
   413	      const importPath = binding.path.parentPath;
   414	      if (importPath && importPath.isImportDeclaration()) {
   415	        const absPath = state.traversalState.importPathResolver(
   416	          importPath.node.source.value,
   417	        );
   418	        if (!absPath) {
   419	          return deopt(
   420	            binding.path,
   421	            state,
   422	            errMsgs.IMPORT_PATH_RESOLUTION_ERROR,
   423	          );
   424	        }
   425	        const [type, value] = absPath;
   426	
   427	        const returnValue =
   428	          type === 'themeNameRef'
   429	            ? evaluateThemeRef(value, importedName, state)
   430	            : evaluateImportedFile(value, importedName, state, bindingPath);
   431	        if (state.confident) {
   432	          if (
   433	            !state.addedImports.has(importPath.node.source.value) &&
   434	            state.traversalState.treeshakeCompensation
   435	          ) {
   436	            importPath.insertBefore(
   437	              t.importDeclaration([], importPath.node.source),
   438	            );
   439	            state.addedImports.add(importPath.node.source.value);
   440	          }
   441	          return returnValue;
   442	        } else {
   443	          deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.IMPORT_FILE_EVAL_ERROR);
   444	        }
   445	      }
   446	    }
   447	
   448	    if (binding && bindingPath && bindingPath.isImportDefaultSpecifier()) {
   449	      deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.IMPORT_FILE_EVAL_ERROR);
   450	    }
   451	
   452	    if (binding && binding.constantViolations.length > 0) {
   453	      return deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.NON_CONSTANT);
   454	    }
   455	
   456	    if (binding && path.node.start < binding.path.node.end) {
   457	      return deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.USED_BEFORE_DECLARATION);
   458	    }
   459	
   460	    if (binding && binding.hasValue) {
   461	      return binding.value;
   462	    } else {
   463	      if (path.node.name === 'undefined') {
   464	        return binding
   465	          ? deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.UNINITIALIZED_CONST)
   466	          : undefined;
   467	      } else if (path.node.name === 'Infinity') {
   468	        return binding
   469	          ? deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.UNINITIALIZED_CONST)
   470	          : Infinity;
   471	      } else if (path.node.name === 'NaN') {
   472	        return binding
   473	          ? deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.UNINITIALIZED_CONST)
   474	          : NaN;
   475	      }
   476	
   477	      const resolved = (path as $FlowFixMe).resolve();
   478	      if (resolved === path) {
   479	        return deopt(path, state, errMsgs.UNDEFINED_CONST);
   480	      } else {
   481	        return evaluateCached(resolved, state);
   482	      }
   483	    }
   484	  }
   485	
   486	  if (path.isUnaryExpression({ prefix: true })) {
   487	    if (path.node.operator === 'void') {
   488	      // we don't need to evaluate the argument to know what this will return
   489	      return undefined;
   490	    }
   491	
   492	    const argument = path.get('argument');
   493	    if (
   494	      path.node.operator === 'typeof' &&
   495	      (argument.isFunction() || argument.isClass())
   496	    ) {
   497	      return 'function';
   498	    }
   499	
   500	    const arg = evaluateCached(argument, state);
   501	    if (!state.confident) return;
   502	    switch (path.node.operator) {
   503	      case '!':
   504	        return !arg;
   505	      case '+':
   506	        return +arg;
   507	      case '-':
   508	        return -arg;
   509	      case '~':
   510	        return ~arg;
   511	      case 'typeof':
   512	        return typeof arg;
   513	      case 'void':
   514	        return undefined;
   515	      default:
   516	        return deopt(
   517	          path,
   518	          state,
   519	          errMsgs.UNSUPPORTED_OPERATOR(path.node.operator),
   520	        );
   521	    }
   522	  }
   523	
   524	  if (path.isArrayExpression()) {
   525	    const arrPath: NodePath<t.ArrayExpression> = path;
   526	    const arr = [];
   527	    const elems: $ReadOnlyArray<NodePath<>> = arrPath.get('elements');
   528	    for (const elem of elems) {
   529	      const elemValue = evaluate(elem, state.traversalState, state.functions);
   530	
   531	      if (elemValue.confident) {
   532	        arr.push(elemValue.value);
   533	      } else {
   534	        elemValue.deopt &&
   535	          deopt(elemValue.deopt, state, elemValue.reason ?? 'unknown error');
   536	        return;
   537	      }
   538	    }
   539	    return arr;
   540	  }
   541	
   542	  if (path.isObjectExpression()) {
   543	    const obj: { [string]: mixed } = {};
   544	    const props: $ReadOnlyArray<
   545	      NodePath<t.ObjectMethod | t.ObjectProperty | t.SpreadElement>,
   546	    > = path.get('properties');
   547	    for (const prop of props) {
   548	      if (prop.isObjectMethod()) {
   549	        return deopt(prop, state, errMsgs.OBJECT_METHOD);
   550	      }
   551	      if (prop.isSpreadElement()) {
   552	        const spreadExpression = evaluateCached(prop.get('argument'), state);
   553	        if (!state.confident) {
   554	          return deopt(prop, state, state.deoptReason ?? 'unknown error');
   555	        }
   556	        Object.assign(obj, spreadExpression);
   557	        continue;
   558	      }
   559	      if (prop.isObjectProperty()) {
   560	        const keyPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty['key']> = prop.get('key');
   561	        let key: string | number | boolean;
   562	        if (prop.node.computed) {
   563	          const {
   564	            confident,
   565	            deopt: resultDeopt,
   566	            reason: deoptReason,
   567	            value,
   568	          } = evaluate(
   569	            keyPath,
   570	            state.traversalState,
   571	            state.functions,
   572	            state.seen,
   573	          );
   574	
   575	          if (!confident) {
   576	            resultDeopt &&
   577	              deopt(resultDeopt, state, deoptReason ?? 'unknown error');
   578	            return;
   579	          }
   580	          key = value;
   581	        } else if (keyPath.isIdentifier()) {
   582	          key = keyPath.node.name;
   583	        } else {
   584	          // TODO: This isn't handling all possible types that `keyPath` could be
   585	          key = (keyPath.node as $FlowFixMe).value;
   586	        }
   587	
   588	        const valuePath: NodePath<> = prop.get('value');
   589	        let value = evaluate(
   590	          valuePath,
   591	          state.traversalState,
   592	          state.functions,
   593	          state.seen,
   594	        );
   595	        if (!value.confident) {
   596	          value.deopt &&
   597	            deopt(value.deopt, state, value.reason ?? 'unknown error');
   598	          return;
   599	        }
   600	        value = value.value;
   601	        obj[key] = value;
   602	      }
   603	    }
   604	    return obj;
   605	  }
   606	
   607	  if (path.isLogicalExpression()) {
   608	    // If we are confident that the left side of an && is false, or the left
   609	    // side of an || is true, we can be confident about the entire expression
   610	    const stateForLeft = { ...state, deoptPath: null, confident: true };

   613	    const leftConfident = stateForLeft.confident;
   614

   616	    const rightPath = path.get('right');
   617	    const right = evaluateCached(rightPath, stateForRight);
   618	    const rightConfident = stateForRight.confident;
   619	
   620	    switch (path.node.operator) {

   732	  if (path.isCallExpression()) {
   733	    const callee = path.get('callee');

   735	    let func;

   815	          func = parsedObj.value[property.node.value];

   845	function evaluateQuasis(
   846	  path: NodePath<t.TaggedTemplateExpression | t.TemplateLiteral>,
   847	  quasis: Array<any>,
   848	  state: State,
   849	  raw: boolean = false,
   850	) {
   851	  let str = '';
   852	
   853	  let i = 0;
   854	  const exprs: $ReadOnlyArray<NodePath<>> = path.isTemplateLiteral()
   855	    ? path.get('expressions')
   856	    : path.isTaggedTemplateExpression()
   857	      ? path.get('quasi').get('expressions')
   858	      : [];
   859	
   860	  // const exprs: Array<NodePath<t.Node>> = path.isTemplateLiteral()
   861	  //   ? path.get('expressions')
   862	  //   : (path as NodePath<t.TaggedTemplateExpression>)
   863	  //       .get('quasi')
   864	  //       .get('expressions');
   865	
   866	  for (const elem of quasis) {
   867	    // not confident, evaluated an expression we don't like
   868	    if (!state.confident) break;
   869	
   870	    // add on element
   871	    str += raw ? elem.value.raw : elem.value.cooked;
   872	
   873	    // add on interpolated expression if it's present
   874	    const expr = exprs[i++];
   875	    if (expr) str += String(evaluateCached(expr, state));
   876	  }
   877	
   878	  if (!state.confident) return;
   879	  return str;
   880	}
   881	
   882	/**
   883	 * Walk the input `node` and statically evaluate it.
   884	 *
   885	 * Returns an object in the form `{ confident, value, deopt }`. `confident`
   886	 * indicates whether or not we had to drop out of evaluating the expression
   887	 * because of hitting an unknown node that we couldn't confidently find the
   888	 * value of, in which case `deopt` is the path of said node.
   889	 *
   890	 * Example:
   891	 *
   892	 *   evaluate(parse("5 + 5")) // { confident: true, value: 10 }
   893	 *   evaluate(parse("!true")) // { confident: true, value: false }
   894	 *   evaluate(parse("foo + foo")) // { confident: false, value: undefined, deopt: NodePath }
   895	 *
   896	 */
   897	
   898	// Track all the imports added to the file, so we don't add them multiple times
   899	// Instead of polluting StateManager with this, we use a WeakMap
   900	// so the logic can be localized this file.

   903	export function evaluate(

   275	        options.classNamePrefix ?? 'x',
   276	        'x',
   277	        'options.classNamePrefix',
   278	      );
   279	
   280	    const configuredImportSources: StyleXStateOptions['importSources'] =
   281	      z.logAndDefault(
   282	        checkImportSources,
   283	        options.importSources ?? [],
   284	        [],
   285	        'options.importSources',
   286	      );
   287	
   288	    const importSources: StyleXStateOptions['importSources'] = [
   289	      name,
   290	      'stylex',
   291	      ...configuredImportSources,
   292	    ];
   293	
   294	    const styleResolution: StyleXStateOptions['styleResolution'] =
   295	      z.logAndDefault(
   296	        z.unionOf3(
   297	          z.literal('application-order'),
   298	          z.literal('property-specificity'),
   299	          z.literal('legacy-expand-shorthands'),
   300	        ),
   301	        options.styleResolution ?? 'property-specificity',
   302	        'property-specificity',
   303	        'options.styleResolution',
   304	      );
   305	
   306	    const unstable_moduleResolution: StyleXStateOptions['unstable_moduleResolution'] =
   307	      z.logAndDefault(
   308	        z.unionOf(z.nullish(), CheckModuleResolution),
   309	        options.unstable_moduleResolution,
   310	        null,
   311	        'options.unstable_moduleResolution',
   312	      );
   313	
   314	    const treeshakeCompensation: StyleXStateOptions['treeshakeCompensation'] =
   315	      z.logAndDefault(
   316	        z.boolean(),
   317	        options.treeshakeCompensation ?? false,
   318	        false,
   319	        'options.treeshakeCompensation',
   320	      );
   321	
   322	    const aliasesOption: StyleXOptions['aliases'] = z.logAndDefault(
   323	      z.unionOf(
   324	        z.nullish(),
   325	        z.objectOf(z.unionOf(z.string(), z.array(z.string()))),
   326	      ),
   327	      options.aliases,
   328	      null,
   329	      'options.aliases',
   330	    );
   331	
   332	    const aliases: StyleXStateOptions['aliases'] =
   333	      aliasesOption == null
   334	        ? aliasesOption
   335	        : Object.fromEntries(
   336	            Object.entries(aliasesOption).map(([key, value]) => {
   337	              if (typeof value === 'string') {
   338	                return [key, [value]];
   339	              }
   340	              return [key, value];
   341	            }),
   342	          );
   343	
   344	    const opts: StyleXStateOptions = {
   345	      aliases,
   346	      classNamePrefix,
   347	      debug,
   348	      definedStylexCSSVariables: {},
   349	      dev,
   350	      enableDebugClassNames,
   351	      enableDebugDataProp,
   352	      enableDevClassNames,
   353	      enableFontSizePxToRem,

   355	      enableMinifiedKeys,
   356	      enableMediaQueryOrder,

   365	      styleResolution,
   366	      test,
   367	      treeshakeCompensation,
   368	      unstable_moduleResolution,
   369	    };
   370	    return opts;
   371	  }
   372	
   373	  get importPathString(): string {
   374	    if (this.importPaths.has('@stylexjs/stylex')) {
   375	      return '@stylexjs/stylex';
   376	    }
   377	    if (this.importPaths.size > 0) {
   378	      // get the first one
   379	      return [...this.importPaths][0];
   380	    }
   381	    return '@stylexjs/stylex';
   382	  }
   383	
   384	  get importSources(): $ReadOnlyArray<string> {
   385	    return this.options.importSources.map((source) =>
   386	      typeof source === 'string' ? source : source.from,
   387	    );
   388	  }
   389	
   390	  importAs(source: string): null | string {
   391	    for (const importSource of this.options.importSources) {
   392	      if (typeof importSource !== 'string' && importSource.from === source) {
   393	        return importSource.as;
   394	      }
   395	    }
   396	    return null;
   397	  }

   411	    }
   412	    const runInj = this.options.runtimeInjection;
   413	    return typeof runInj === 'string' ? { from: runInj } : runInj || null;

   444	  get fileNameForHashing(): null | string {
   445	    const filename = this.filename;
   446	    const themeFileExtension =
   447	      this.options.unstable_moduleResolution?.themeFileExtension ?? '.stylex';
   448	
   449	    if (
   450	      filename == null ||
   451	      !matchesFileSuffix(themeFileExtension)(filename) ||
   452	      this.options.unstable_moduleResolution == null
   453	    ) {
   454	      return null;
   455	    }
   456	
   457	    switch (this.options.unstable_moduleResolution.type) {
   458	      case 'haste':
   459	        return path.basename(filename);
   460	      default:
   461	        return this.getCanonicalFilePath(filename);
   462	    }
   463	  }
   464	
   465	  getPackageNameAndPath(
   466	    filepath: string,
   467	  ): null | [+packageName: string, +packageDir: string] {
   468	    const folder = path.dirname(filepath);
   469	
   470	    const hasPackageJSON = fs.existsSync(path.join(folder, 'package.json'));
   471	    if (hasPackageJSON) {
   472	      try {
   473	        const packageJson = JSON.parse(
   474	          fs.readFileSync(path.join(folder, 'package.json'), 'utf8'),
   475	        );
   476	        const name = packageJson.name;
   477	        return [name, folder];
   478	      } catch (err) {
   479	        console.error(err);
   480	        return null;
   481	      }
   482	    } else {
   483	      if (folder === path.parse(folder).root || folder === '') {
   484	        return null;
   485	      }
   486	      return this.getPackageNameAndPath(folder);
   487	    }
   488	  }
   489	
   490	  getCanonicalFilePath(filePath: string): string {
   491	    const pkgNameAndPath = this.getPackageNameAndPath(filePath);
   492	    if (pkgNameAndPath == null) {
   493	      const rootDir = this.options.unstable_moduleResolution?.rootDir;
   494	      if (rootDir != null) {
   495	        return path.relative(rootDir, filePath);
   496	      }
   497	      const fileName = path.relative(path.dirname(filePath), filePath);
   498	      return `_unknown_path_:${fileName}`;
   499	    }
   500	    const [packageName, packageDir] = pkgNameAndPath;
   501	    return `${packageName}:${path.relative(packageDir, filePath)}`;
   502	  }
   503	
   504	  importPathResolver(importPath: string): ImportPathResolution {
   505	    const sourceFilePath = this.filename;
   506	    if (sourceFilePath == null) {
   507	      return false;
   508	    }
   509	
   510	    switch (this.options.unstable_moduleResolution?.type) {
   511	      case 'commonJS': {
   512	        const aliases = this.options.aliases;
   513	        const themeFileExtension =
   514	          this.options.unstable_moduleResolution?.themeFileExtension ??
   515	          '.stylex';
   516	        if (!matchesFileSuffix(themeFileExtension)(importPath)) {
   517	          return false;
   518	        }
   519	        const resolvedFilePath = filePathResolver(
   520	          importPath,
   521	          sourceFilePath,
   522	          aliases,
   523	        );
   524	        return resolvedFilePath
   525	          ? ['themeNameRef', this.getCanonicalFilePath(resolvedFilePath)]
   526	          : false;
   527	      }
   528	      case 'haste': {
   529	        const themeFileExtension =
   530	          this.options.unstable_moduleResolution.themeFileExtension ??
   531	          '.stylex';
   532	        if (!matchesFileSuffix(themeFileExtension)(importPath)) {
   533	          return false;
   534	        }
   535	        return ['themeNameRef', addFileExtension(importPath, sourceFilePath)];
   536	      }
   537	      case 'experimental_crossFileParsing': {
   538	        const aliases = this.options.aliases;
   539	        const themeFileExtension =
   540	          this.options.unstable_moduleResolution.themeFileExtension ??
   541	          '.stylex';
   542	        if (!matchesFileSuffix(themeFileExtension)(importPath)) {
   543	          return false;
   544	        }
   545	        const resolvedFilePath = filePathResolver(
   546	          importPath,
   547	          sourceFilePath,
   548	          aliases,
   549	        );
   550	        return resolvedFilePath ? ['filePath', resolvedFilePath] : false;
   551	      }
   552	      default:
   553	        return false;
   554	    }
   555	  }
   556	
   557	  addStyle(
   558	    style: [

   560	      (

   566	            ltr: string,
   567	          }
   568	      ),
   569	      number,
   570	    ],

   620	              nameHint: 'inject',

    10	import type { InjectableStyle, StyleXOptions } from '../common-types';

    12	import { convertStyleToClassName } from '../utils/convert-to-className';
    13	import { arrayEquals } from '../utils/object-utils';
    14	import { sortAtRules, sortPseudos } from '../utils/rule-utils';
    15	
    16	export type ClassesToOriginalPaths = {
    17	  +[className: string]: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    18	};
    19	
    20	export type ComputedStyle = null | $ReadOnly<
    21	  [string, InjectableStyle, ClassesToOriginalPaths],
    22	>;
    23	
    24	// The classes in this file are used to represent objects that
    25	// can be compiled into one or CSS rules.
    26	//
    27	// These are thin wrappers around the "values" in Raw Style Objects
    28	// with all the metadata needed to compile them into CSS.
    29	export interface IPreRule {
    30	  compiled(options: StyleXOptions): $ReadOnlyArray<ComputedStyle>;
    31	  equals(other: IPreRule): boolean;
    32	}
    33	
    34	export type AnyPreRule = NullPreRule | PreRule | PreRuleSet;
    35	
    36	export class NullPreRule implements IPreRule {
    37	  compiled(_options: StyleXOptions): [null] {
    38	    return [null];
    39	  }
    40	
    41	  equals(other: IPreRule): boolean {
    42	    return other instanceof NullPreRule;
    43	  }
    44	}
    45	
    46	export class PreRule implements IPreRule {
    47	  +property: string;
    48	  +value: string | number | $ReadOnlyArray<string | number>;
    49	  +keyPath: $ReadOnlyArray<string>;
    50	
    51	  constructor(
    52	    property: string,
    53	    value: string | number | $ReadOnlyArray<string | number>,
    54	    keyPath?: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    55	  ) {
    56	    this.property = property;
    57	    this.keyPath = keyPath ?? [];
    58	    this.value = value;
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  get pseudos(): $ReadOnlyArray<string> {
    62	    const unsortedPseudos = this.keyPath.filter((key) => key.startsWith(':'));
    63	    return sortPseudos(unsortedPseudos);
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  get atRules(): $ReadOnlyArray<string> {
    67	    const unsortedAtRules = this.keyPath.filter((key) => key.startsWith('@'));
    68	    return sortAtRules(unsortedAtRules);
    69	  }
    70	
    71	  get constRules(): $ReadOnlyArray<string> {
    72	    // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
    73	    return this.keyPath.filter((key) => key.startsWith('var(--'));
    74	  }
    75	
    76	  compiled(
    77	    options: StyleXOptions,
    78	  ): $ReadOnlyArray<[string, InjectableStyle, ClassesToOriginalPaths]> {
    79	    const [_key, className, rule] = convertStyleToClassName(
    80	      [this.property, this.value],
    81	      this.pseudos ?? [],
    82	      this.atRules ?? [],
    83	      this.constRules ?? [],
    84	      options,
    85	    );
    86	
    87	    return [[className, rule, { [className]: this.keyPath }]];
    88	  }
    89	
    90	  equals(other: IPreRule): boolean {
    91	    if (!(other instanceof PreRule)) {
    92	      return false;
    93	    }
    94	
    95	    const valuesEqual =
    96	      Array.isArray(this.value) && Array.isArray(other.value)
    97	        ? arrayEquals(this.value, other.value)
    98	        : this.value === other.value;
    99	
   100	    return (
   101	      this.property === other.property &&
   102	      valuesEqual &&
   103	      arrayEquals(this.pseudos, other.pseudos) &&
   104	      arrayEquals(this.atRules, other.atRules)
   105	    );
   106	  }
   107	}
   108	
   109	export class PreRuleSet implements IPreRule {
   110	  +rules: $ReadOnlyArray<PreRule | NullPreRule>;
   111	
   112	  constructor(rules: $ReadOnlyArray<PreRule | NullPreRule>) {
   113	    this.rules = rules;
   114	  }
   115	
   116	  static create(
   117	    rules: $ReadOnlyArray<PreRule | NullPreRule | PreRuleSet>,
   118	  ): AnyPreRule {
   119	    const flatRules = rules.flatMap((rule) =>
   120	      rule instanceof PreRuleSet ? rule.rules : [rule],
   121	    );
   122	    if (flatRules.length === 0) {
   123	      return new NullPreRule();
   124	    }
   125	    if (flatRules.length === 1) {
   126	      return flatRules[0];
   127	    }
   128	    return new PreRuleSet(flatRules);
   129	  }
   130	
   131	  compiled(options: StyleXOptions): $ReadOnlyArray<ComputedStyle> {
   132	    const styleTuple: $ReadOnlyArray<ComputedStyle> = this.rules
   133	      .flatMap((rule) => rule.compiled(options))
   134	      .filter(Boolean);
   135	    return styleTuple.length > 0 ? styleTuple : [null];
   136	  }
   137	
   138	  equals(other: IPreRule): boolean {
   139	    if (!(other instanceof PreRuleSet)) {
   140	      return false;
   141	    }
   142	    if (this.rules.length !== other.rules.length) {
   143	      return false;
   144	    }
   145	    return arrayEquals(this.rules, other.rules, (a, b) => a.equals(b));
   146	  }
   147	}

     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.
     3	 *
     4	 * This source code is licensed under the MIT license found in the
     5	 * LICENSE file in the root directory of this source tree.
     6	 *
     7	 * @flow strict
     8	 */
     9	
    10	'use strict';
    11	
    12	import type { InjectableStyle, StyleXOptions } from '../common-types';
    13	import { defaultOptions } from './default-options';
    14	
    15	import generateLtr from '../physical-rtl/generate-ltr';
    16	import generateRtl from '../physical-rtl/generate-rtl';
    17	import getPriority from './property-priorities';
    18	
    19	const THUMB_VARIANTS = [
    20	  '::-webkit-slider-thumb',
    21	  '::-moz-range-thumb',
    22	  '::-ms-thumb',
    23	];
    24	
    25	function buildNestedCSSRule(
    26	  className: string,
    27	  decls: string,
    28	  pseudos: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    29	  atRules: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    30	  constRules: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    31	): string {
    32	  const pseudo = pseudos.filter((p) => p !== '::thumb').join('');
    33	  const combinedAtRules = atRules.concat(constRules);
    34	
    35	  let selectorForAtRules =
    36	    `.${className}` +
    37	    combinedAtRules.map(() => `.${className}`).join('') +
    38	    pseudo;
    39	
    40	  if (pseudos.includes('::thumb')) {
    41	    selectorForAtRules = THUMB_VARIANTS.map(
    42	      (suffix) => selectorForAtRules + suffix,
    43	    ).join(', ');
    44	  }
    45	
    46	  return combinedAtRules.reduce(
    47	    (acc, combinedAtRules) => `${combinedAtRules}{${acc}}`,
    48	    `${selectorForAtRules}{${decls}}`,
    49	  );
    50	}
    51	
    52	export function generateCSSRule(
    53	  className: string,
    54	  key: string,
    55	  value: string | $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    56	  pseudos: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    57	  atRules: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    58	  constRules: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    59	  options: StyleXOptions = defaultOptions,
    60	): InjectableStyle {
    61	  const pairs: $ReadOnlyArray<[string, string]> = Array.isArray(value)
    62	    ? value.map((eachValue) => [key, eachValue])
    63	    : [[key, value]];
    64	
    65	  const ltrPairs = pairs.map((pair) => generateLtr(pair, options));
    66	  const ltrDecls = ltrPairs.map((pair) => pair.join(':')).join(';');
    67	
    68	  const rtlDecls = pairs
    69	    .map((pair) => generateRtl(pair, options))
    70	    .filter(Boolean)
    71	    .map((pair) => pair.join(':'))
    72	    .join(';');
    73	
    74	  const ltrRule = buildNestedCSSRule(
    75	    className,
    76	    ltrDecls,
    77	    pseudos,
    78	    atRules,
    79	    constRules,
    80	  );
    81	  const rtlRule = !rtlDecls
    82	    ? null
    83	    : buildNestedCSSRule(className, rtlDecls, pseudos, atRules, constRules);
    84	
    85	  const priority =
    86	    getPriority(key) +
    87	    pseudos.map(getPriority).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) +
    88	    atRules.map(getPriority).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) +
    89	    constRules.map(getPriority).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
    90	
    91	  return { priority, ltr: ltrRule, rtl: rtlRule };
    92	}

    32	  options: $ReadOnly<{

    34	    ...
    35	  }>,

     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.
     3	 *
     4	 * This source code is licensed under the MIT license found in the
     5	 * LICENSE file in the root directory of this source tree.

     9	
    10	import type { RawStyles, StyleXOptions, TStyleValue } from '../common-types';
    11	
    12	import flatMapExpandedShorthands from './index';
    13	import { lastMediaQueryWinsTransform } from 'style-value-parser';
    14	import * as messages from '../messages';
    15	
    16	import {
    17	  NullPreRule,
    18	  PreRule,
    19	  PreRuleSet,
    20	  type AnyPreRule,
    21	  type IPreRule,
    22	} from './PreRule';
    23	
    24	export function flattenRawStyleObject(
    25	  style: RawStyles,
    26	  options: StyleXOptions,
    27	): $ReadOnlyArray<$ReadOnly<[string, IPreRule]>> {
    28	  let processedStyle = style;
    29	  try {
    30	    processedStyle = options.enableMediaQueryOrder
    31	      ? lastMediaQueryWinsTransform(style)
    32	      : style;
    33	  } catch (error) {
    34	    throw new Error(messages.INVALID_MEDIA_QUERY_SYNTAX);
    35	  }
    36	  return _flattenRawStyleObject(processedStyle, [], options);
    37	}
    38	
    39	export function _flattenRawStyleObject(
    40	  style: RawStyles,
    41	  keyPath: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    42	  options: StyleXOptions,
    43	): Array<$ReadOnly<[string, AnyPreRule]>> {
    44	  const flattened: Array<$ReadOnly<[string, AnyPreRule]>> = [];
    45	  for (const _key in style) {
    46	    const value = style[_key];
    47	    const key: string = _key.match(/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/)
    48	      ? _key.slice(4, -1)
    49	      : _key;
    50	
    51	    // Default styles
    52	    if (
    53	      value === null ||
    54	      typeof value === 'string' ||
    55	      typeof value === 'number'
    56	    ) {
    57	      const pairs: $ReadOnlyArray<[string, TStyleValue]> =
    58	        flatMapExpandedShorthands([key, value], options);
    59	      for (const [property, value] of pairs) {
    60	        if (value === null) {
    61	          flattened.push([property, new NullPreRule()]);
    62	        } else {
    63	          flattened.push([
    64	            property,
    65	            new PreRule(
    66	              property,
    67	              value,
    68	              keyPath.includes(key)
    69	                ? keyPath.map((k) => (k === key ? property : k))
    70	                : [...keyPath, property],
    71	            ),
    72	          ]);
    73	        }
    74	      }
    75	      continue;
    76	    }
    77	
    78	    // Fallback Styles
    79	    if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    80	      // Step 1: Expand properties to its constituent parts
    81	      // Collect the various values for each value in the array
    82	      // that belongs to the same property.
    83	      const equivalentPairs: {
    84	        [string]: Array<null | string | number>,
    85	      } = {};
    86	      for (const eachVal of value) {
    87	        const pairs = flatMapExpandedShorthands([key, eachVal], options);
    88	        for (const [property, val] of pairs) {
    89	          if (Array.isArray(val)) {
    90	            if (equivalentPairs[property] == null) {
    91	              equivalentPairs[property] = [...val];
    92	            } else {
    93	              equivalentPairs[property].push(...val);
    94	            }
    95	          } else if (equivalentPairs[property] == null) {
    96	            equivalentPairs[property] = [val];
    97	          } else {
    98	            equivalentPairs[property].push(val);
    99	          }
   100	        }
   101	      }
   102	      // Deduplicate
   103	      Object.entries(equivalentPairs)
   104	        // Remove Nulls
   105	        .map(([property, values]) => [
   106	          property,
   107	          [...new Set(values.filter(Boolean))],
   108	        ])
   109	        // Deduplicate and default to null when no values are found
   110	        .map(([property, values]) => [
   111	          property,
   112	          values.length === 0 ? null : values.length === 1 ? values[0] : values,
   113	        ])
   114	        // Push to flattened
   115	        .forEach(([property, value]) => {
   116	          if (value === null) {
   117	            flattened.push([property, new NullPreRule()]);
   118	          } else {
   119	            flattened.push([
   120	              property,
   121	              new PreRule(
   122	                property,
   123	                value,
   124	                keyPath.includes(_key)
   125	                  ? keyPath.map((k) => (k === _key ? property : k))
   126	                  : [...keyPath, property],
   127	              ),
   128	            ]);
   129	          }
   130	        });
   131	      continue;
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    // Object Values for properties. e.g. { color: { hover: 'red', default: 'blue' } }
   135	    if (
   136	      typeof value === 'object' &&
   137	      !key.startsWith(':') &&
   138	      !key.startsWith('@')
   139	    ) {
   140	      const equivalentPairs: { [string]: { [string]: AnyPreRule } } = {};
   141	      for (const condition in value) {
   142	        const innerValue = value[condition];
   143	
   144	        const pairs = _flattenRawStyleObject(
   145	          { [key]: innerValue },
   146	          keyPath.length > 0 ? [...keyPath, condition] : [key, condition],
   147	          options,
   148	        );
   149	        for (const [property, preRule] of pairs) {
   150	          if (equivalentPairs[property] == null) {
   151	            equivalentPairs[property] = { [condition]: preRule };
   152	          } else {
   153	            equivalentPairs[property][condition] = preRule;
   154	          }
   155	        }
   156	      }
   157	      for (const [property, obj] of Object.entries(equivalentPairs)) {
   158	        const sortedKeys = Object.keys(obj); //.sort();
   159	        const rules: Array<AnyPreRule> = [];
   160	        for (const condition of sortedKeys) {
   161	          rules.push(obj[condition]);
   162	        }
   163	        // If there are many conditions with `null` values, we will collapse them into a single `null` value.
   164	        // `PreRuleSet.create` takes care of that for us.
   165	        flattened.push([property, PreRuleSet.create(rules)]);
   166	      }
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    // Object Values for pseudos and at-rules. e.g. { ':hover': { color: 'red' } }
   170	    if (
   171	      typeof value === 'object' &&
   172	      (key.startsWith(':') || key.startsWith('@'))
   173	    ) {
   174	      const pairs = _flattenRawStyleObject(value, [...keyPath, _key], options);
   175	      for (const [property, preRule] of pairs) {
   176	        flattened.push([key + '_' + property, preRule]);
   177	      }
   178	    }
   179	  }
   180	  return flattened;
   181	}
